  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8a13e249-23c9-4979-8c7d-5279e497ecbf'

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer16387810362121274504">When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone. <br/>Everyone said she was a fraud, that she was just making it up. <br/>I'd really like to know why the hell a person would make up a thing like that.<br/><br/>Written with the snap, glitter and wit of The Girl's Guide to Hunting and Fishing, God-Shaped Hole is a memorable, poignant love</span>
  <span id="freeText16387810362121274504" style="display:none">When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone. <br />Everyone said she was a fraud, that she was just making it up. <br />I'd really like to know why the hell a person would make up a thing like that.<br /><br />Written with the snap, glitter and wit of The Girl's Guide to Hunting and Fishing, God-Shaped Hole is a memorable, poignant love story that will leave you weeping with laughter. It is told in the wry, vulnerable voice of Beatrice "Trixie" Jordan who replies to a personal ad, "If your intentions are pure I am seeking a friend for the end of the world."<br /><br />In doing so, she meets Jacob Grace, a charming, effervescent thirty-something writer, a free spirit who is a passionate seeker of life. He possesses his own turn of phrase and ways of thinking and feeling that dissonantly harmonize with Trixie's off-center vision as they roller coaster through the joys and furies of their wrenching romance. Along the way they try to come to terms with the hurt brought about by their distant fathers who, in different ways, forsook them.<br /><br />This story will prove so touching you will rush to share it with a friend or loved one or even a stranger.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16387810362121274504" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I'm guessing she named it God-Shaped Hole, and the novel we read is in fact Trixie's journal. <br/>That's my interpretation.<br/><br/>I like the symbolics of it and <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I'm guessing she named it God-Shaped Hole, and the novel we read is in fact Trixie's journal. <br />That's my interpretation.<br /><br />I like the symbolics of it and the fact that Trixie has a lot more in her life to happen, we only got to see a small portion of it. How many more journals will she fill in...<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

You will understand the "God-Sha<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">It has religious references and while the main character had a Catholic schooling, she is in fact far from religious. You will understand the "God-Shaped hole" reference and meaning once you read the book. It is an amazing story and I highly recommend reading this book.     <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547093842" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17156982700088524443"><b>5 INCREDIBLE STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6edaee91-230a-48db-99e7-e87a27180df8_zpsab62a996.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807590.jpg' alt=' photo 6edaee91-230a-48db-99e7-e87a27180df8_zpsab62a996.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>What can I say about this book? It kept me up all night reading. It made me think. It made me re-evaluate my own life. It moved me. It destroyed me.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/35417bac-8500-4f1d-9455-1bc6986a59d5_zpse40a2d4f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807591.jpg' alt=' photo 35417bac-8500-4f1d-9455-1bc6986a59d5_zpse40a2d4f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Beatrix (Trixie) and Jacob meet by an ad. It’s silly. Jacob put it in the paper, just because... and Trixie answered. <br/><b>
  <blockquote>If your intentions are pure<br/>I’m seeking a friend <br/>For the end <br/>Of the world.</blockquote>
</b> Some people are just meant to meet. Meant to know each other, be in each others lives. Thats how it is with Jacob Grace and Tri</span>
  <span id="freeText17156982700088524443" style="display:none"><b>5 INCREDIBLE STARS!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/6edaee91-230a-48db-99e7-e87a27180df8_zpsab62a996.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807590.jpg" alt=" photo 6edaee91-230a-48db-99e7-e87a27180df8_zpsab62a996.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What can I say about this book? It kept me up all night reading. It made me think. It made me re-evaluate my own life. It moved me. It destroyed me.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/35417bac-8500-4f1d-9455-1bc6986a59d5_zpse40a2d4f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807591.jpg" alt=" photo 35417bac-8500-4f1d-9455-1bc6986a59d5_zpse40a2d4f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Beatrix (Trixie) and Jacob meet by an ad. It’s silly. Jacob put it in the paper, just because... and Trixie answered. <br><b>
  <blockquote>If your intentions are pure<br>I’m seeking a friend <br>For the end <br>Of the world.</blockquote>
</b> Some people are just meant to meet. Meant to know each other, be in each others lives. Thats how it is with Jacob Grace and Trixie. They are just meant to be. From the first time they meet, they both know it. Jacob is different than any man Trixie has ever met. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I got the impression Jacob was an odd person. And I mean that as the best possible compliment I could give a guy.</blockquote>
</b><br>Jacob feels something with Trixie he as never felt. He knows she is it for him.<br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>“Here’s the thing. I feel like we grew in the same womb or something. Like we’ve been connected from the beginning by blood and veins. Siamese soul lovers, if there could ever be such a thing.”</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/3ddbb1d4-1034-4f55-874d-91d731a57264_zps7c221578.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807592.jpg" alt=" photo 3ddbb1d4-1034-4f55-874d-91d731a57264_zps7c221578.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jacob is a writer working on his novel called <i>Hallelujah</i>, and Trixie makes her own jewelry and sells it to high end stores. I loved these two together. The time they spent together, the things they talked about. Everything. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/96b3dd49-1352-4af4-9fc5-0ce63a53e8c8_zpse002e9d1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807593.jpg" alt=" photo 96b3dd49-1352-4af4-9fc5-0ce63a53e8c8_zpse002e9d1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>“We’re all searching for something to fill up what I like to call that big, God-shaped hole in our souls. Some people use alcohol, or sex, or their children, or food, or money, or music, or heroin. A lot of people even use the concept of God itself. I could go on and on. I used to know a girl who used shoes. She had over two-hundred pairs. But it’s all the same thing, really. People, for some stupid reason, think they can escape their sorrows.”</blockquote>
</b> They are able to communicate about life, love, their families, hopes, dreams, fears. Trixie has many fears... her biggest fear being death. Jacob, not so much. One thing he is afraid of... <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Everyone’s afraid of something.” I said.<br>“Okay then,” he said, trying to think of something quickly. “I’m afraid of sleeping another night without you. How’s that?”</blockquote>
</i> I fell in love with Jacob Grace. He is a man unlike any other. He has issues, mostly with his father, but he is the sweetest, kindest, most soulful character. He is a lover, a dreamer, passionate, just amazing. You can’t help but adore him. He really is ‘it’ for Trixie. No matter what this couple goes through, there is never a question about it. They were made for each other. They have this intense connection, you just can’t explain it. You can feel it. Jacob is everything Trixie has ever wanted, what she’s been looking for her entire life. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/08624c1a-d9ba-44cd-b255-7de8b14c0f8c_zps5f9d6052.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807594.jpg" alt=" photo 08624c1a-d9ba-44cd-b255-7de8b14c0f8c_zps5f9d6052.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Trixie and Jacob have a plan. They are going south once his book sells, getting out of LA. They have hopes, dreams, aspirations. Beautiful, beautiful plans. But you know what they say...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/37f2911e-f67f-4ec1-a3e6-9b20c0f042c7_zpsec2e39bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807595.jpg" alt=" photo 37f2911e-f67f-4ec1-a3e6-9b20c0f042c7_zpsec2e39bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>These two characters are not perfect- they are far from it. But they are absolutley 100% perfect for one another. They make mistakes throughout their journey, but they always find their way back to one another.<br><b>
  <blockquote>Bottom line: It’s okay to screw up as long as you keep trying. The key is to keep trying.</blockquote>
</b><br>I am gonna stop right here... I don’t want to spoil the ending, and I can’t really talk about it right now. You just have to read this one for yourself. Is it devastating at times? Yes. Will your heart break into a million little pieces while reading? Yes. Is it one of the best, most well written books I’ve ever read? Yes. Will I ever forget Jacob and Trixie’s story? No. Never. <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>
    <i>“The days will always be brighter because he existed.<br>The nights will always be darker because he's gone.<br>And no matter what anybody says about grief, and about time healing all wounds, the truth is, there are certain sorrows that never fade away until the heart stops beating and the last breath is taken.” Cue my uncontrollable SOBBING! OMG YES I SOBBED!!!! </i>
  </b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/ef3c8631-88e0-4d36-a543-ef9471362bbd_zpse0073664.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807596.jpg" alt=" photo ef3c8631-88e0-4d36-a543-ef9471362bbd_zpse0073664.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book was incredible. Tiffanie Debartolo may be the most talented author I’ve ever had the pleasure of reading. Her books are like nothing else. I can’t describe how I’m feeling right now, but Trixie and Jacob’s journey was beautiful, inspiring, heartbreaking... This is one of those ‘More than 5 star’ books. One thing is for certain- while reading this book you will <b>feel</b>. It’s one of those books that will cause you to become an emotional wreck. Hot mess. But it’s okay. It’s worth it. A truly phenomenal and unforgettable read. <br><br>I would recommend this book, and Tiffanie’s other book: How to Kill a Rockstar to anyone, but you should know, her books should come with a warning:<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/11bf7f41-5624-419f-ad56-64aad01ca3de_zpseff007a5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411303i/807597.jpg" alt=" photo 11bf7f41-5624-419f-ad56-64aad01ca3de_zpseff007a5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17156982700088524443" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer637897238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6883454146504080641"><br/><br/><b> “You wanna know how to make God laugh?. Tell him your plans” </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380365474i/717548._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Dear Diary,<br/><br/>Yes, I know. I usually write in Spanish but guess what? I am making this entry public. Why, you ask? Well, I want to review a book and this one felt so personal that I wanted to tell you how I feel after reading it. <br/><br/>This book… Nope, not this book. This author… OMG, holly hell this author!!! She’ll make you change your life, she’ll make you believe this life is worth it, she’ll make you FEEL. How important is that? How many </span>
  <span id="freeText6883454146504080641" style="display:none"><br><br><b> “You wanna know how to make God laugh?. Tell him your plans” </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380365474i/717548._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dear Diary,<br><br>Yes, I know. I usually write in Spanish but guess what? I am making this entry public. Why, you ask? Well, I want to review a book and this one felt so personal that I wanted to tell you how I feel after reading it. <br><br>This book… Nope, not this book. This author… OMG, holly hell this author!!! She’ll make you change your life, she’ll make you believe this life is worth it, she’ll make you FEEL. How important is that? How many people read just because they want to FEEL something? <br><br>That quote about making plans? So fitting! And so true, right? I love it how we all make our plans but sometimes that upper hand is just laughing at us because we can make as many plans as we want, that won’t mean they will happen.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424863i/847272._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book tells us the story about Trixie &amp; Jacob. Jacob puts an ad on the newspaper because he wants to meet someone ‘special’ and Trixie reads it and she decides to call. Crazy, huh? Sometimes you just need to do crazy things to be happy and Trixie did the right thing because having someone like Jacob in your life is one of the best things that could happen to a girl.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”We are all searching for something to fill up what I like to call that big, God-shaped hole in our souls”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I don’t really want to spoil this one for you, I am trying to express my emotions about books when reviewing, instead of giving away too much info and specially with books like this one. I want everyone to go blind. To experience. To feel!<br><br>Tiffanie has the power to create the BEST heroes EVER! Ok, they are not the hottest guys with the best 6 pack but who needs that? Seriously! I want special heroes, intelligent ones, loving ones, I don’t need two hotties falling in love just because. And Tiffanie knows how to deliver this.<br><br><b>This is a journey about having a relationship, about appreciating what life is giving you, about living every single second, about understanding, about happiness and over all this is a book about love.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424863i/847273.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is nothing else I could say without spoiling the story so I will shut up now. But I beg everyone to read Tiffanie’s books. They are the BEST. EVER. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>You can’t wait forever for something, and then say it’s too late when the time finally comes</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Listen to this song while reading this, PRETTY PLEASE! As Jacob would say, <b> ‘A good song can save your life. Don’t ever forget it.’ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=d9ljye9gnNY">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=d9ljy...</a><br><br><b>Keep going ladies, ALWAYS keep going! That is what this book is about</b>… Enjoy the ride!<br><br><b>PLEASE DO NOT OPEN THE SPOILER IF YOU HAVEN’T READ HOW TO KILL A ROCK STAR &amp; GOD-SHAPED HOLE </b>. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ So, you remember MY Loring??? Yes, MINE. Ok, you remember on page 366 of HTKARS when Eliza sees him with a girl? Yes, that girl who made jewelry? I know, right? Loring &amp; Trixie are TOGETHER!!! Go back to HTKARS and read from page 366 onwards and enjoy the crying!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>THANKS DAWN &amp; SHARON for making me read this one, I owe you BIG TIME. x<br></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_667487306" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/667487306" />
    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/667487306?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer667487306" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5816643469991518334"><b>4 depressing stars.****Review completed August 8, 2013</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429157i/859416._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo b3a80ea8-3bf2-41ec-949f-2e64f2b8d781_zpsa9442d9d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429157i/859417._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo d29925fe-7741-4287-9ab7-4fc908292483_zps05651bb8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859418.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_m46880S9Bv1rqpem4o1_500_zps463e1a81.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"(…) I think we are God. We all have that inside of us. And I believe we go on after we've turned to dust. Our souls, I mean."<br/>(…)<br/>"A search. We're all searching for something to fill up what I like to call that big God-shaped hole in our souls. Some people use alcohol, or sex, or their children, or food, or money, or music, or heroin. A lot of people even use the concept of God itself. (…)"</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859419.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_m6pbgcQJlF1roq4e2o1_500_zpse8e29dbb.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I have decided to not review God-Shaped Ho</span>
  <span id="freeText5816643469991518334" style="display:none"><b>4 depressing stars.****Review completed August 8, 2013</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429157i/859416._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo b3a80ea8-3bf2-41ec-949f-2e64f2b8d781_zpsa9442d9d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429157i/859417._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo d29925fe-7741-4287-9ab7-4fc908292483_zps05651bb8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859418.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m46880S9Bv1rqpem4o1_500_zps463e1a81.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"(…) I think we are God. We all have that inside of us. And I believe we go on after we've turned to dust. Our souls, I mean."<br>(…)<br>"A search. We're all searching for something to fill up what I like to call that big God-shaped hole in our souls. Some people use alcohol, or sex, or their children, or food, or money, or music, or heroin. A lot of people even use the concept of God itself. (…)"</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859419.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6pbgcQJlF1roq4e2o1_500_zpse8e29dbb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I have decided to not review God-Shaped Hole. The following paragraph about loss is all you get from me regarding this story. Also, I think that my pictures and gifs as well as the quotes and the poem do speak for themselves. I would like to add one thing though. While it is very obvious that God-Shaped Hole deals with fear, loss and the meaning of life, it also touches another sensitive subject matter: God &amp; religion. This leads me to my conclusion that I'm not able to review God-Shaped Hole without getting personal. I have learned my lesson, and I'm not willing anymore to put my little self out there in the open.<br><br>Whatever you decide, God-Shaped Hole is a great book and so worth reading. Just make sure that you are in the right frame of mind before you delve into this heartbreaking story because it is not a book to be enjoyed. It's one of those to be experienced, and I'm pretty sure it's going to leave a hole in your heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Real annihilation happens from the inside out.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>As expected the writing is eye-catching and great but God-Shaped Hole is frigging depressing. I knew all that when I read the blurb and yet…it's Tiffanie…you need to read her books, and I hope she will be writing a lot more in the (near) future. She has a magnificent talent to engage me in a story and to keep me <i>there</i>. That's the true beauty and force of words; when they are powerful enough to haunt you for a long time after you've closed the book. Reading her thoughtful and poignant words is moving but at the same time also very upsetting. Everyone has experienced loss in their life. After all it's a natural process and unavoidable. Yet what makes it even sadder are the circumstances, the how and when loss occurs. The <i>why.</i> It's final. What remains are memories that, in the best case, will make you smile and in the worst case will aggravate your (almost) unbearable pain and grief. And the biggest bullshit of all is that time will heal your wounds. That's such nonsense and not true. You learn to live with loss and pain. And over time your pain fades and blurs but it doesn't go away completely. The open wound festers for a while and closes eventually, however, the scar is what will cause you trouble for the rest of your life. There remains a dull pain that flares up from time to time depending on how moody you are. Like rainy weather that is going to trouble your joints, you know? As long as you're alive that little pain will be your constant companion, and a part of that hole in your heart. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"That's why I love you," he said. "You try and act so tough, you think you're so damn hopeless and godless and faithless, but you don't fool me. People without hope aren't tormented by the world the way you are. People without hope don't give a shit. But I see it in you, in the way you look at things, even in the way you look at me sometimes, like I'm the coolest fucking guy in the universe, and I know it's in there. Reverence. Belief. <b>Something.</b> You have a lot more faith than you own up to. You just don't want to be let down. But I'm not going to let you down again. Not if I can help it."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Come dance with me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859420.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mpqoldjo3A1svg2vso1_500_zpsbf1e49fa.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859421.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mf5sptcZh61rv0zuco1_500_zps24eda46d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Jacob," I said, "do you think there's anything in life that can fill up the hole? And not only fill it up, but keep it filled?"<br>"That's the real trick, isn't it?" he said incisively. "It's easy to plant a seed and sprinkle it with water, but once the sun scorches the ground, and the earth soaks up all the moisture, you're left with nothing but a thirsty little flower trying desperately to make it out of the dirt."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859422.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_meobah2ttg1qdunk8o1_500_zps1ee89467.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380303168ra/687753.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfz9srQEE01rmdeaso1_500_zps7f121f85.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"Last spring, Jacob and I went to Catalina for the day. We hiked about three miles up a trail, to a bluff overlooking the whole island. We snuck off the path and made our way into this tiny meadow that was covered with wild flowers. Jacob spotted two butterflies there, right at the edge of the field. They were just hanging out, fluttering from one flower to another, and he couldn't take his eyes off them. I mean he was <b>mesmerized</b> by the damn things." I paused to regain some composure--remembering a day like that had the power to thoroughly wreck me. "We followed those two stupid insects around for over an hour, and do you want to know <b>why?"</b> I wiped my nose with the sleeve of my fifteen-hundred dollar suit. "Because Jacob was curious about what butterflies <b>did,</b> that's why. So don't tell me Jacob was <b>reckless.</b> Jacob was <b>not</b> reckless. Jacob just wanted to <b>feel</b> things. He wanted to <b>live,</b> something you wouldn't know the first thing about."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389442ra/750532.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mjggh4qZWA1s0nzhno1_500_zpsddadb9c3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429157i/859423._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 379b042e-07e9-4732-9cde-322c67cb5421_zpsbe7d7afa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429157ra/859424.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m473eughL91qbb77eo1_500_zpsf9caa908.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <blockquote>You are the music, in the <br>symphony of life. <br><br>You are the music in the peace <br>solitude and stillness of the <br>early a.m., for you are the <br>song in my heart. <br><br>You are the music on an ocean's front, <br>for you are the roar of the waves, <br>the power of the sea, <br>and the salt in the air. <br><br>You are the music amidst a crowd <br>and the chorus of city sounds <br>for that is my song, <br>and you are the music. <br><br>You are the music in my thoughts <br>of each new day, and the last image <br>I glimpse, as my eyes are <br>closed upon a feathered pillow. <br><br>You are the music, In that secret place <br>called sleep. I search for you through <br>all the songs of life. It is you that <br>I search for, through shades of darkness <br>and clouds of cotton. <br><br>When I think of you, the music is always and <br>forever. Every moment of my life. And, when <br>the final sleep does come and if there is music, <br>I shall think of you. <br><br>© Joe Fazio </blockquote>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396734ra/765041.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_md2xnp5m4n1qj73e2o1_500_zps49196aac.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"If your intentions are pure I'm seeking a friend for the end of the world."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br>Recommended read.<br><br><br><br>P.S. I hope that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Jacob Grace has found his <i>Grace</i> land. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>P.P.S. Yes, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/113791.How_to_Kill_a_Rock_Star" title="How to Kill a Rock Star by Tiffanie DeBartolo" rel="nofollow noopener">How to Kill a Rock Star</a> is by far the better book. Again, you should read her books.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1090558295" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1090558295?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18952257-god-shaped-hole">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1090558295" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6157401139610774830"><blockquote>
  <b>When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone. <br/>Everyone said she was a fraud, <br/>that she was just making it up. <br/>I'd really like to know why the hell a person would make up a thing like that.</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414683852i/11677379.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This is the sort of book that you just need to read, without knowing too much about it. I have read this author's other book and really liked it but this one has a different feel to it.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>Trixie," he said. "Do you mind if I call you Trixie?"</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414683814i/11677374.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Most bo</span>
  <span id="freeText6157401139610774830" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone. <br>Everyone said she was a fraud, <br>that she was just making it up. <br>I'd really like to know why the hell a person would make up a thing like that.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414683852i/11677379.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is the sort of book that you just need to read, without knowing too much about it. I have read this author's other book and really liked it but this one has a different feel to it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Trixie," he said. "Do you mind if I call you Trixie?"</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414683814i/11677374.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Most books that have references to music are usually a win/win situation for me. I love music and try and get to concerts on a regular basis.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I've only discovered four things that make life worth living for me. <br>My work is one of them."<br>"What are the other three?"<br>"Music, books and sex," I said. "Not necessarily in that order."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414683814i/11677375._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>I discovered Nick Drake when I was in school but hadn't listened to him in years. His music was full of grief and torment and truth ...</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414685745i/11677555._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I have heard of most of the musicians mentioned in the book. If you don't know names like Nick Drake, Miles Davis, Jeff Buckley, Harry Chapin, check them out. On a side note my first time visiting the States, nearly 25 years ago, with my then boyfriend (now Himself) we took the train from NYC out to Long Island to visit Huntington and try and find the resting place of Harry. Himself was the big fan, not me ... aaah, the things you do for love!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414683814i/11677376._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Don't waste your time with fear."<br>"Fear won't keep you safe from being hurt."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414685745i/11677556.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Still waters run deep...</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414685745i/11677557.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I put off reading this one for a long time but Sharon and Karen's reviews finally got my ass in gear to read it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414685745i/11677558.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <a title="Em Lost In Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11166121-em-lost-in-books"><img alt="Em Lost In Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522743986p2/11166121.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2377239682?book_show_action=true">Apr 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Em Lost In Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Em Lost In Books" href="/user/show/11166121-em-lost-in-books">Em Lost In Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34139890-god-shaped-hole">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11166121-em-lost-in-books?shelf=stand-alone-read">stand-alone-read</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2377239682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9934750860230090167"><b>
  <i>Don't waste your time with fear.. Fear won't keep you safe from being hurt.</i>
</b><br/><br/>took it's sweet time to really get started but once it did this story was hard to let go. Beatrice and Jacob were not perfect but they were perfect for each other. Came close to break off but soon realized that it's foolish to hurt the person you love because it makes you more sad and feel worse.<br/><br/>A bittersweet love story. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_426150560" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/426150560" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/426150560?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=made-me-emotional">made-me-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer426150560" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15444162030576781278"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>If your intentions are pure, I'm seeking a friend for the end of the world.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>Best...personal...ad...ever.<br/><br/>Tiffanie DeBartolo - her words slay me. This wasn't quite as good as her other book <i>How to Kill a Rock Star</i>, but I still can't believe this was her first novel. For a first effort, it was quite impressive. Hell, I can't believe more people haven't read her work. There is something about the way this woman puts words together which makes my brain hurt, but in a good way. We move from</span>
  <span id="freeText15444162030576781278" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>If your intentions are pure, I'm seeking a friend for the end of the world.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />Best...personal...ad...ever.<br /><br />Tiffanie DeBartolo - her words slay me. This wasn't quite as good as her other book <i>How to Kill a Rock Star</i>, but I still can't believe this was her first novel. For a first effort, it was quite impressive. Hell, I can't believe more people haven't read her work. There is something about the way this woman puts words together which makes my brain hurt, but in a good way. We move from poetic to witty...from heartfelt to heartbreaking. I am in awe of how the words on the page have me smiling one moment and crying the next.<br /><br />The very first lines of the book should have anyone intrigued about what's going to happen.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />If you don't feel something when you are finished reading one of DeBartolo's books, I honestly don't know what to say. Be it anger, sorrow, joy, frustration, satisfaction...there should be some sort of emotion rolling around in your brain by the time you close the pages. I already knew how this book was going to end and still found myself emotional. <br /><br /><b>Jacob</b> - How could anyone not love the offbeat tormented soul that was Jacob? He was the being which gave this book a life.<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Don't tell me Jacob is reckless. Jacob is <u>not</u> reckless. Jacob just wants to <u>feel</u> things. He wants to <u>live</u>, something you wouldn't know the first thing about."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><b>Beatrice (Trixie)</b> - She's unsettled, unsatisfied, and looking for a way out.<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Maybe that was the dreamer in me. I try to find meaning anywhere I can. It's the only way I know how to validate my existence.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br /><br />Two broken people brought together by fate or coincidence? Even I had to stop and wonder about this.<br /><br />This story was more than just a love story. It was a life story. We watched real people live real lives. We saw the good, the bad, and the ugly. I can't tell you much more than this. I HAVE to be vague. Just read the book and you'll get why this non-review says nothing other than what you will find out right at the start.<br /><br />Minor complaints I have would revolve around a few repetitive scenes, some slight editing issues, and a few moments where the tone mirrored <i>How to Kill a Rock Star</i> in brief flashes. I don't have too much to complain about though. I know that it can be off-putting to see some of the constant complaining from the characters about SoCal and I get that, since I'm a native Cali girl myself, but DeBartolo gave props to San Francisco, so I was somewhat pacified with that turn of events. O.o<br /><br />This book captured my heart and ripped it out at the same time.<br /><br />I loved Jacob and Trixie. I shall miss them.<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You're the world's muse, Trixie."<br />"I just want to be your muse."<br />"Done."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15444162030576781278" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2297280483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15171078507798486435">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a> <br/><br/>The warning signs were shining like G.D. beacons that I would not enjoy <i>God-Shaped Hole</i>. <br/><br/>#1 – The blurb by Dave Eggers told me to expect a main character who was a 27-year old female Holden Caulfield. There are two types of people in this world – those who love Holden Caulfield and those who hate him. <b>I DESPISE HOLDEN CAULFIELD.</b><br/><br/>#2 – The blurb was by DAVE EGGERS. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1926591064?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>YUCK</a>.<br/><br/>#3 – The foreward claimed the inspiration for this story came from J</span>
  <span id="freeText15171078507798486435" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a> <br><br>The warning signs were shining like G.D. beacons that I would not enjoy <i>God-Shaped Hole</i>. <br><br>#1 – The blurb by Dave Eggers told me to expect a main character who was a 27-year old female Holden Caulfield. There are two types of people in this world – those who love Holden Caulfield and those who hate him. <b>I DESPISE HOLDEN CAULFIELD.</b><br><br>#2 – The blurb was by DAVE EGGERS. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1926591064?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">YUCK</a>.<br><br>#3 – The foreward claimed the inspiration for this story came from Jeff Buckley’s album <i>Grace</i>, which no one should deny <b>is</b> a truly great album, but seriously . . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519666683ra/25127053.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>How fucking cliché can one book get? <br><br>#4 – Since I am an old lady who was familiar with Jeff Buckley before “Shrek” created the milkshake that brought all the girls to his yard, I was pretty sure I knew how this would turn out without ever reading the synopsis.<br><br>#5 – Then I read the first paragraph and it totally confirmed that everything I thought about how this would end was 100% accurate.<br><br>So why did I read it? Because my real-life book buddy told me to, we are generally of one mind when it comes to our reactions to stories and she promised this would fall into the “love it” rather than “hate it” category. <br><br>And on any other day there’s a solid chance I <i>could</i> have enjoyed this more as I am most definitely a “right place and right time reader.” Unfortunately, even if I was in the mood for super saccharine love, there would have been one ginormo hindrance to my love-fest: <b>BEATRICE</b>. Now, I am a self-proclaimed asshole so I am definitely not opposed to characters who are assholes. Beatrice took it to a whole new level. From wanting to tell complete strangers that they were fat so they shouldn’t be eating chips as a snack, to how everything smelled weird to her delicate senses, to people’s decorating styles of the ugliest she’d ever seen, to sales girls that must have cutlets in their bras to give them cleavage to how people were too stupid to understand her jewelry designs, Beatrice had nothing nice to say most of the time and I found her to be insufferable. Much like Holden Caulfield, I guess. <br><br>But to those of you who can either find her relatable or at least not so awful you are hoping her boyfriend will die and ruin her life, you might discover that this was the literary equivalent of the Miss Dior commercials. Do you know what I’m talking about? Natalie Portman is all gorgeous running down the beach with smokey eyes in a soaking wet ballgown . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519666683ra/25127054.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Or with a fabulous red lip . . . .<br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519666683ra/25127055.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Where a love story is captured from start to finish in 30 seconds and things are both great . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519666683ra/25127056.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then not so great when he’s all “I love you” and she’s all . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519666683ra/25127057.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Which is “prove it” but for some reason I could only find it in Spanish and then she gets super shovey, but then in another one they’re all . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519666683ra/25127058.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And I am just maybe too old for a story like that and that makes me saaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaad because I don’t want to be old and also . . . . <br><br><a href="https://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519666683ra/25127059.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But I didn’t like it and it didn’t make me have any feelings (aside from annoyance, but I feel that feeling nearly all of the time) so it only gets 2 Stars : (<br></span>

<div id="review_786130566" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/786130566" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/786130566?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6972914-karen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer786130566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer231231236258903598">Fuck, that hurt. And my highlighter is out of ink.<br/>Bloody sensational. If I can find the words, review will follow...<br/><br/><b>5 SOLID STARS ★★★★★</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Couples/roshambo.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642309._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo roshambo.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i> “Just knowing you exist changed the world for me.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>How to review this amazing book? Well, I guess I will start off by saying that it will probably be one of my favorite books of the year. I will also say that I felt just the same about Tiffanie DeBartolo’s other book, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/113791.How_to_Kill_a_Rock_Star' title='How to Kill a Rock Star by Tiffanie DeBartolo' rel='nofollow noopener'>How to Kill a Rock Star</a>. So, perhaps it’s just a connection I feel with he</span>
  <span id="freeText231231236258903598" style="display:none">Fuck, that hurt. And my highlighter is out of ink.<br>Bloody sensational. If I can find the words, review will follow...<br><br><b>5 SOLID STARS ★★★★★</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Couples/roshambo.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642309._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo roshambo.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “Just knowing you exist changed the world for me.” </i>
</b><br><br>How to review this amazing book? Well, I guess I will start off by saying that it will probably be one of my favorite books of the year. I will also say that I felt just the same about Tiffanie DeBartolo’s other book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/113791.How_to_Kill_a_Rock_Star" title="How to Kill a Rock Star by Tiffanie DeBartolo" rel="nofollow noopener">How to Kill a Rock Star</a>. So, perhaps it’s just a connection I feel with her writing style? Maybe. Regardless, she is a fantastic writer… and I’ll gladly read anything she puts out in the future. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Couples/black-amp-white-hands-love-photography-Favimcom-253142.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642310.jpg" alt=" photo black-amp-white-hands-love-photography-Favimcom-253142.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “I fall in love too easily."</i>
</b><br><br>Ok. That said, if you are considering this book, just keep in mind that happily ever afters are relative things. They are subjective, and they are rare. And sometimes you have to take the bad with the good in order to have the good at all. I know that sounds cryptic, but I don’t quite know how to express my thoughts on this without saying too much. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/7430728.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642311._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7430728.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> He didn’t say anything, he just devoured me with a freedom I never knew could be contained in a kiss.</i>
</b><br><br>I will not say much about the story itself. This is one you just have to experience first hand. It is a romance. In the true sense of the word. And, I mean life altering love here. Romeo and Juliet kind of love. Rare and precious. The kind of love that breathes life into a dead heart; the kind that fills the soul. The kind that only comes once in a lifetime. The kind you’ll let destroy you. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/3A847751-350C-4C52-AE68-D6012CD01C80.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343341i/11642337.jpg" alt=" photo 3A847751-350C-4C52-AE68-D6012CD01C80.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> It was a record called Seven Steps to Heaven by Miles Davis. He told me that if it didn’t bring tears to my eyes when I listened to it, he couldn’t be my friend.</i>
</b><br><br>So the question is…. would you risk it? Would you venture in, knowing that to experience this completeness… this filling of your soul, that you could lose it all someday? Some say, that it is better to have always been poor than to once have been rich, and then lose it all.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/the-fortune-teller.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642312._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo the-fortune-teller.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “I’m afraid of everything. Fear of being alone, fear of being hurt, fear of being made a fool of, fear of failure... Still, I think all my fears bleed from one big one…DEATH.” </i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/1A9773BB-52AB-4C2E-8CAC-265D71659F5D.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413878337i/11575970._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1A9773BB-52AB-4C2E-8CAC-265D71659F5D.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t think so though. In the case of love… to never know it, is to always be poor. And that is <b>not</b> acceptable. And that is just how I feel about reading books like this. I knew the book would be painful, and it was. But I feel all the richer for experiencing it. No regrets.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/el-tornillo-que-te-falta-roshambo-1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642313._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo el-tornillo-que-te-falta-roshambo-1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Committing suicide so as not to be murdered is the worst reason I've ever heard of to die. ” </i>
</b><br><br>These two characters, Beatrice Jordan and Jacob Grace, have earned a permanent place in my heart. I cannot express how much I loved them both. They met through a personal ad…<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/laweekly_logo.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343731i/11642377._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo laweekly_logo.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“If your intentions are pure, <br>I'm seeking a friend <br>for the end <br>of the world.”</i>
</b> <br><br>and were instantly connected. I am in awe of what they shared. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Dear Trixie,<br>Will you come to Memphis with me?<br>A) Yes<br>B) No<br>C) I'd go anywhere with you because you fuck like a goddamn fire hose.<br>D) You're an asshole and I never want to see you again.<br>Circle ONLY ONE and give it back to me when you're done eating.<br>Love, J” </i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/Graceland_sign.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642314._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Graceland_sign.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And the quotes… my God, I have never highlighted so many quotes in my life. I wasn’t joking about my highlighter being out of ink. (except that I read on a Kindle ;)<br><br><b>
  <i> “People without hope aren’t tormented by the world like you are. People without hope don’t give a shit. But I see in you, in the way you look at things, even in the way you look at me sometimes, like I’m the coolest fucking guy in the universe, and I know it’s there. Reverence.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/Hallelujah1929.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642315._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Hallelujah1929.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The writing was witty, sexy and often profound. I frequently laughed out loud. The supporting characters were real, quirky and just fantastic. I wanted to know them all… well except for Chip. I loved everything about this book. Well, except maybe… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the end <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><b>
  <i> “I don’t believe in anything. But I believe in the possibility of everything.”</i>
</b><br><br>So my final question is… can your true soul mate be a fictional character? If so, than I think I found mine. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/1bce7071-9766-4324-b307-904f7cc107c6.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642316.png" alt=" photo 1bce7071-9766-4324-b307-904f7cc107c6.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/daniel-bederov-long-hair.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414843343i/11698525.jpg" alt=" photo daniel-bederov-long-hair.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>One might accuse me of bias, as I automatically categorize anyone whose semen tastes like lemon meringue pie as extraordinary, but sex aside, I was wholly impressed.</i>
</b><br><br>That’s all I have to say.<br><br>Now go read the effing book, and don’t give me any sob stories about not doing sad… only HEA’s! Suck it up and drink the poison! You can thank me later!!!<br><br><b>
  <i> “In my soul, there’s just a big hole where God’s supposed to be.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/4542332116_f00b9962b9_z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414343059i/11642317._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4542332116_f00b9962b9_z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>5 SOUL FILLING STARS!!!!!</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="231231236258903598" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_331651428" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/331651428" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/331651428?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=books-that-cross-the-line">books-that-cross-the-line</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer331651428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16968289536009320389"> Frickin' book....<br/><br/>Frickin' tearjerker...<br/><br/>and...frickin' cliffhanger.<br/><br/><b>DON'T</b> read this book...or do...yes do...it's soooo good!<br/><br/>Ok rant over...here's the review:<br/><br/>Beatrice is tired of the same ol' same ol' dating scene so when she sees an ad that says: <br/><br/><i>"If you're intentions are pure <br/>I'm seeking a friend <br/>for the end <br/>of the world."</i><br/><br/>Well, her interests are peaked and she just can't resist answering it. That's how she meets Jacob Grace. <br/><br/>No news flash that I love emotional books but this book <i>killed</i> me just </span>
  <span id="freeText16968289536009320389" style="display:none"> Frickin' book....<br /><br />Frickin' tearjerker...<br /><br />and...frickin' cliffhanger.<br /><br /><b>DON'T</b> read this book...or do...yes do...it's soooo good!<br /><br />Ok rant over...here's the review:<br /><br />Beatrice is tired of the same ol' same ol' dating scene so when she sees an ad that says: <br /><br /><i>"If you're intentions are pure <br />I'm seeking a friend <br />for the end <br />of the world."</i><br /><br />Well, her interests are peaked and she just can't resist answering it. That's how she meets Jacob Grace. <br /><br />No news flash that I love emotional books but this book <i>killed</i> me just like I knew it would. If you're a fan of <i>How To Kill A Rock Star</i>, you will love this book. It's all that and more. And I know it's a pain because this book is not available as an ebook but just buy the book! And I really want to know...Why hasn't this woman written more?? <br /><br />Both Beatrice (aka Trixie) and Jacob have problems and they are a bit different...Jacob especially but he <i>is</i> a writer! They both have father problems and on top of that, when Beatrice was young, a fortune teller told her she would meet the love of her life but she would lose him to tragedy. Well, right there you know something awful is going to happen and I hated waiting for the bomb to drop. Ugh!! <br /><br />Some of the things that Beatrice and Jacob said and did were a bit over the top and it took me a while to get into the story but somehow they reeled me in. I loved how they both knew all these music references and authors. But then, they both were jerks...again especially Jacob. I didn't really blame Beatrice for acting the way she did. But in a way, this just made their relationship more real because they weren't perfect. <br /><br />There's a great cast of characters in the book as well. Both Beatrice's and Jacob's best friends, Kat and Pete, were priceless! And I really loved Sara. Jacob's Mom and Beatrice's family really rounded things out. <br /><br />So when the bomb actually hits, it's really bad. It makes me sick just thinking about it. I actually thought that something else (<i>anything else</i>) would happen. On top of that, when the book ends, it leaves you hanging. You don't know what's going to happen but I guess that's how it's suppose to be. <br /><br />I loved it and I hated it but I will <b>never</b> regret reading it.<br /><br />**on a side note, I spent my summer vacation in Santa Monica and I LOVED all the references...well, except the "bomb" one. <br /> <br /><br />Favorite quotes:<br /><br />♥ "God, you sleep a lot. I must've really worn you out last night."<br /><br />♥ "We're all searching for something to fill up what I like to call that big, God-shaped hole in our souls."<br /><br />♥ <i>Dear Trixie,<br />Will you come to Memphis with me?<br />A) Yes<br />B) No<br />C) I'd go anywhere with you because you f*ck like a goddamn fire hose. <br />D) You're an *sshole and I never want to see you again.<br />Circle ONLY ONE and give it back to me when you're done eating.<br />Love,J</i><br /><br />♥ "Contrary to what you seem to think, <i>Rosalita</i>, it's been a while for me."<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16968289536009320389" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_9307472" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/9307472" />
    <a title="Lewis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/629538-lewis"><img alt="Lewis" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/9307472?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2007</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lewis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lewis" href="/user/show/629538-lewis">Lewis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer9307472" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4929930980317933184">There's never been a book that infuriated me more than <i>God-Shaped Hole</i>. Not because it's "edgy," not because it's "insightful" or "daring." It is, quite honestly, the complete opposite. It is a book about a narcissistic written by a woman so full of her own ideas about true love (none of which ring true in the simplest of terms) that it wouldn't at all be surprising if she had written that the character of Beatrice suddenly turned to the Heavens and yelled, "It's me! It's me! Tiffanie!"<br/><br/>And so <i>Go</i></span>
  <span id="freeText4929930980317933184" style="display:none">There's never been a book that infuriated me more than <i>God-Shaped Hole</i>. Not because it's "edgy," not because it's "insightful" or "daring." It is, quite honestly, the complete opposite. It is a book about a narcissistic written by a woman so full of her own ideas about true love (none of which ring true in the simplest of terms) that it wouldn't at all be surprising if she had written that the character of Beatrice suddenly turned to the Heavens and yelled, "It's me! It's me! Tiffanie!"<br /><br />And so <i>God-Shaped Hole</i> exists, about a lonely woman with a craving between her legs responding to a personal ad in the paper. It is a fluke (or as Tiffanie keeps berating us with, "fate"), where Beatrice meets the charming, too-good-to-be-true Jacob. They hit it off and, before long, are living together, complaining about the same shithole they live in (Los Angeles) and about its shallow inhabitants (though they are just as shallow as anyone they consistently condescend to). <br /><br />They have there ups-and-downs, fights that come off like petty tenth grade drama because the other just won't open up their mouth and say something. It's a continuity issue in terms of Jacob's character, who is written like a God-like martyr who knows all the right things to say, knows just how to swirly his pelvis so Beatrice gets pleasured like she never has before, and even calls her "Trixie." Ain't that just cute? But he'll go into mood swings and say things that aren't his character; they don't flesh him out as a character, the interactions just feel like plot contrivances.<br /><br />And then there's that foreshadowing that rips any sort of suspense or emotion right from the awkwardly phrased final pages. From the very front cover ("When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone...") to the "tear jerking" finalé, we're supposed to fall in love with these characters that are so smitten with themselves and the other that they don't realize they are still as selfish and asinine as anyone else. The characters are not deep, they aren't organic. <i>God-Shaped Hole</i> is just another bout of soap opera-lite odes to the great, mysterious force called "love," and this one just happens to be one of the most inane of all.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4929930980317933184" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
