<div id="review_773853810" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/773853810" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/773853810?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer773853810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9127221977504247253"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386634231i/7410315.jpg' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> "You want to know how to make God laugh? Tell him your plans."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386640655i/7412635.jpg' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>Where to even begin? <br/>I feel like I have so much to say but can't get it out in a coherent sentence. </b><br/><br/>When I read a book (and decide to review it) I usually have a process I go through. As I go through the story, I have a sort of... outline in my head of what I want to say. So my reviews are usually a reflection of what I thought and felt throughout the whole entire book, while I was 'in the moment.' With <i>God-Shaped Hole</i>, I</span>
  <span id="freeText9127221977504247253" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386634231i/7410315.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> "You want to know how to make God laugh? Tell him your plans."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386640655i/7412635.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Where to even begin? <br>I feel like I have so much to say but can't get it out in a coherent sentence. </b><br><br>When I read a book (and decide to review it) I usually have a process I go through. As I go through the story, I have a sort of... outline in my head of what I want to say. So my reviews are usually a reflection of what I thought and felt throughout the whole entire book, while I was 'in the moment.' With <i>God-Shaped Hole</i>, I finished it without having any clue of what the hell I was going to talk about. All I did while reading this book was <i>
  <b>feel.</b>
</i> This is a story that makes you think about <i>everything</i> and <i>nothing</i> at the same time. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> It was a story about people with dreams. Dreams that never come true.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386640701ra/7412683.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Anyone that knows me and has seen my shelf knows what type of books I read. I'm not too picky but I usually go for a story with some angst and a HEA... and by HEA I mean they get married, have kids, live in a place where there is world peace and die of old age together holding hands. Sounds corny and predictable but I go to my books to escape. Not to see more of the problems I have can find the real world. <br>However, there comes a day when I decide: <i>You know what, Destini? You haven't suffered in a while. </i><br>And that's where <i>God-Shaped Hole</i> comes into play. I'm just going to let everyone know right now, it's <b>depressing.</b> I mean, you really have to be in the right frame of mind to start this one. Don't let that discourage you, though! It's a <i>
  <b>beautiful</b>
</i> story. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386639588ra/7412073.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote>“It seemed cruelly unfair to me, even then, how fast your life can change before you have an opportunity to rethink your choices. <b>We should get second chances on the big stuff.</b> We should come equipped with erasers attached to the tops of our heads. Like pencils. We should be able to flip over and scribble away mistakes, at least once or twice during the duration of our existence, <b>especially in matters of life and death.”</b> </blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386640919ra/7412795.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I didn't choose this book to escape into. I chose it because I felt I could gain some perspective on a few things. And I did. This story... it's not like others. You're reading about this couple's life, which should sound extremely boring, but it wasn't. Everything was so <i>
  <b>genuine</b>
</i> and I was immediately pulled in. <br>I was <b>there.</b> In the book, experiencing everything. I cried when they did, suffered when they suffered, laughed when they laughed, loved them as they loved each other... I <b>felt</b> it all. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386639446i/7411943.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Trixie and Jacob... I don't think I could have describe a more imperfectly perfect couple. They truly were <i>
  <b>siamese soul lovers.</b>
</i> Trixie makes the list for my top heroines but Jacob... he was the one that really stole my heart. <br>He was such a kind, gentle soul but so full of life. I can't put it in better words than this:<br><i>
  <blockquote>[his eyes] ... they were older, wearier than his age let on. But I sensed in them a splash of irony, too; a proud acceptance of the fact that life can be a bitch sometimes, that some people feel things too deeply.</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386639280i/7411849.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He was who he was and I loved him for it. Jacob was far from perfect and made some bad decisions but ultimately, he was good at heart. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386640176i/7412412._SY540_.jpg" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote> "You try and act so tough, you think you're so damn <b>hopeless</b> and <b>godless</b> and <b>faithless</b>, but you don't fool me. People without hope aren't tormented by the world they way you are. <b>People without hope don't give a shit.</b> But I see it in you, in the way you look at things, even in the way you look at me sometimes, like I'm the coolest fucking guy in the universe, and I know it's in there. Reverence. Belief. <b>Something.</b> You have a lot more faith than you own up to." </blockquote>
</i><br>This story deals with religion and faith but it doesn't make up the book. If anything, I would describe it more as discovering the meaning in life. The meaning for everything. The <i>reason</i> for anything being the way it is, why we are the way we are... and why some things happen to us. <br><br>Even though this is a tough read, it wasn't all depressing. Trixie and Jacob had a dry humor that had me wiping tears away. <br>And when it's all over and you look back, it's sad, nobody can deny that, but there are also good memories. Happy things that you remember. That leave you smiling. <br><i>
  <blockquote> "I know it's late but," he paused, "would it be all right if I came over?"<br>"Right now?"<br>"Yeah."<br>"Jacob," I said, "how long have you been waiting to ask me that?"<br>"Who knows?" he said, more to himself than to me. <br>"Maybe all my life."</blockquote>
</i><br><b>I would definitely recommend reading this book. It's a story that'll stay with you forever, that will still have you <i>feeling</i> years later. </b><br>I've said everything in the best way I can but honestly, this is a book that needs to be experienced. <br>My song for <i>God-Shaped Hole:</i> <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WIF4_Sm-rgQ" rel="nofollow noopener">Hallelujah</a><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386641076ra/7412876.gif" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9127221977504247253" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_761215886" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/761215886" />
    <a title="Lo Bookfrantic" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14746493-lo-bookfrantic"><img alt="Lo Bookfrantic" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1450644315p2/14746493.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/761215886?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lo Bookfrantic" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lo Bookfrantic" href="/user/show/14746493-lo-bookfrantic">Lo Bookfrantic</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14746493-lo-bookfrantic?shelf=arc-review-ng">arc-review-ng</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14746493-lo-bookfrantic?shelf=funny-as-shit">funny-as-shit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14746493-lo-bookfrantic?shelf=in-the-feels">in-the-feels</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer761215886" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17641107708472241219"><b>4★★★★Stars<br/><br/>Genre: <i>Contemporary Romance</i><br/>Type: <i>Standalone</i><br/>POV: <i>First Person – Female</i><br/><br/><br/><blockquote><i>"If your intentions are pure I'm seeking a friend for the end of the world."</i></blockquote>
<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488574762ra/22132758.gif' width='500' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Beatrice aka "Trixie" Jordan was a free spirit kind of person; an artist at heart. She occupied her time making and designing her own jewelry and she made it from the heart. They were precious to her. Her talent was well known and very fast her business bloom big time. Trixie loved music and wasn't the type of person that could deal with peop</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17641107708472241219" style="display:none"><b>4★★★★Stars<br><br>Genre: <i>Contemporary Romance</i><br>Type: <i>Standalone</i><br>POV: <i>First Person – Female</i><br><br><br><blockquote><i>"If your intentions are pure I'm seeking a friend for the end of the world."</i></blockquote>
<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488574762ra/22132758.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beatrice aka "Trixie" Jordan was a free spirit kind of person; an artist at heart. She occupied her time making and designing her own jewelry and she made it from the heart. They were precious to her. Her talent was well known and very fast her business bloom big time. Trixie loved music and wasn't the type of person that could deal with peoples crap. She just didn't feel that she had time to deal with people if she didn't have to and so she focus on what she liked best, books, music, making jewelry and having sex. The essentials of course (my type of girl) hehe.<br><br><br>Jacob Grace was a writer with dreams and super cool character. He was simple yet complicated because he knew what he liked and he was extremely honest. He spoke his mind and heart and that's why his circle of friends adored him. He was also a free spirit that loved to live in the moment making memories.<br><br><br>One silly newspaper add changed both of these two forever. They knew from the first day they met that they were meant for each other; they have found their soul mates in each other. Their relationship was super cool, fun, hot, real, and adventurous. <br><br><br><blockquote><i>“Here’s the thing. I feel like we grew in the same womb or something. Like we’ve been connected from the beginning by blood and veins. Someone soul lovers, if there could ever be such a thing.”</i></blockquote>
<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488574762ra/22132760.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I really liked all the side characters from heroine best friend who was hilarious and hero's circle of friends. Jacob struggle internally for not growing up with a father; things happened and he felt he couldn't opened up so he leaves Trixie for few weeks without telling her. Oh boy was she angry and was I pissed off?! Hell to the yes. I was so angry at him it really upset me. However when he comes back it was hard not to forgive him, still he left a sour taste in my mouth because I don't forget easily haha. The words he said; the things he did though made him so unique and special. <br><br><blockquote><i>“We’re all searching for something to fill up what I like to call that big, God-shaped hole in our souls."</i></blockquote>
<br><br>The end; well ever since the beginning and based on blurb and title I already knew how this was going to end. So when it happened I didn't cry; however the aftershocks effects were painful, the memories, what could have been gutted me till no end. I kid you not I cried in the shower for an hour, I cried myself to sleep that night and I'm crying as I'm typing this right now…but Shhh don't judge whatever. Haha!<br><br><blockquote><i>"Everyone feels that void. Everyone who has the balls to look inside themselves, anyway. It's what life's all about…A search."</i></blockquote>
<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1465089030ra/19312670.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488574762ra/22132759.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is unique, the writing is phenomenal, the characters are awesome, there are sexy times, hilarious stuff I laughed so hard reading this book. I can honestly say it is not for everyone though because if you are looking for a "HEA" you best stay away from this book. One thing I know for sure is that this story will stay with me forever.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488574762ra/22132762.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1488574762ra/22132761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>★★I found the E-Copy on Netgalley, OMG I was so excited when I saw it with new cover and everything but same story otherwise I think I would have not been able to finish my paperback copy this year haha★★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450044604i/17371090._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="https://craziesrusbookblog.wordpress.com//" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434387282i/15214674._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450764696i/17467413.jpg" width="" height="50" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </a><a href="https://twitter.com/CraziesRus" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450633462i/17450183.png" width="60" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="https://www.pinterest.com/craziesrus/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img <div id="review_537619160" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537619160" />
    <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday"><img alt="Ash Wednesday" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379043440p2/10484016.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537619160?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ash Wednesday" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ash Wednesday" href="/user/show/10484016-ash-wednesday">Ash Wednesday</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=holy-shit-moments">holy-shit-moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=paperback">paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10484016-ash-wednesday?shelf=goddamn-onions">goddamn-onions</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537619160" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10216424753487467312"><i>
  <b>4.5 STARS<br/><br/>"God is a concept by which we measure our pain"<br/>-'God', John Lennon </b>
</i><br/><br/>Tiffanie DeBartolo wrote 2 books, and if any of your friends recommend either this or <i>How to Kill A Rock Star</i>, take it as a compliment. Because TDB's books are those that won't coddle you with puff pastry dialogue or feed you saccharine lines and emotional scenes that you would squee over on your updates with a Zooey Deschanel gif (something I'm guilty of once in a while, surely). When someone recommends you a book o</span>
  <span id="freeText10216424753487467312" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>4.5 STARS<br><br>"God is a concept by which we measure our pain"<br>-'God', John Lennon </b>
</i><br><br>Tiffanie DeBartolo wrote 2 books, and if any of your friends recommend either this or <i>How to Kill A Rock Star</i>, take it as a compliment. Because TDB's books are those that won't coddle you with puff pastry dialogue or feed you saccharine lines and emotional scenes that you would squee over on your updates with a Zooey Deschanel gif (something I'm guilty of once in a while, surely). When someone recommends you a book of hers, it means someone thinks you're a rock star.<br><br>The story starts with Trixie Jordan (whose name reminds me of Tracy Jordan from 30Rock, lol) answering Jacob Grace's personal ad looking for someone "with pure intentions, a friend for the end of the world". This sets off the starting point of an emotionally charged and tumultuous affair where the "Bad Guy" is a city and the goal is escape.<br><br>If Laini Taylor's prose reminds me of <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hKLpJtvzlEI" rel="nofollow noopener">Clint Mansell</a>, Tiffanie DeBartolo's is (pre-electric) Bob Dylan. A poet for the everyday. And in true DeBartolo fashion, <i>God-Shaped Hole</i> offers to take you on a trip that spans from the philosophical to the mundane, from heartbreak to laughter, from feeling you can conquer everything to asking why we even bother. This book will deliver you to that place in your brain, the one that makes the white noise sound in the day to day, the one we ignore unless we're high or drunk because sometimes it gets too overwhelming for a Wednesday afternoon. <br><br>Not bad for a debut novel.<br><br><i>God-Shaped Hole</i> feels like the avante-garde first born who doesn't let the world dictate his behavior while HTKARS was the crowd pleaser who went on to win the Oscar. I could draw a million analogies between the 2 books but after reading this, I do feel <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[HTKARS was a bit of a compromise. Not necessarily a bad thing. I would imagine the author, receiving much griping about the implausibility of the second half of HTKARS, would offer this book as an answer (and it IS the perfect answer to that issue)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> gripes that I personally had about that wonderful book. But by the end of GSH, I still had the same gripe about the same issue.<br><br>I'm such a fickle child, I know.<br><br>I'm gonna be going off to find a new book to fill the <i>God-Shaped Hole</i> hole inside me. A futile search with a 99.9% chance of failure because none of them will be written in the Tiffanie vernacular.<br><br>I'll end my review with a quote that should be included in the goodreads TOS, forced down the throat of every new author that trolls on the reviewers' comment thread:<br><br><b>
  <i>To Jacob, the act of critiquing art was essentially imprecise. That's why he didn't read reviews on anything he liked, be it a book, a movie, a record. He believed that any work an artist puts forth which contains the truth as he or she sees it is worthy of consideration, and any commentary of the work beyond that is nothing more than pure individual opinion and should not be considered relevant to the work itself.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409881ra/803016.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10216424753487467312" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16205457-shannon-the-show-stopper?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16205457-shannon-the-show-stopper?shelf=paperback">paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16205457-shannon-the-show-stopper?shelf=always-a-keeper">always-a-keeper</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer784857718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5332016631077637664"><b>5+++++ STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Sometimes the most consequential moments in my life originate from a state of completely witless human auto-pilot."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>Jacob places this personal add at the newspaper where he works:<br/><br/><a href='http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reviews/97567ddc-d97f-46e0-9e20-b1f9c85e6ff5_zps4d25f8f5.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391471919i/8394885._SX540_.png' alt=' photo 97567ddc-d97f-46e0-9e20-b1f9c85e6ff5_zps4d25f8f5.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Beatrice answers his add on whim... <br/><br/>It's fate bringing these two Siamese soul lovers together and what a couple they are. <br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I feel like we grew in the same womb or something. Like we've been connected from the beginning by blood and veins. Siamese soul lovers..."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>Beatrice, the narra</span>
  <span id="freeText5332016631077637664" style="display:none"><b>5+++++ STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Sometimes the most consequential moments in my life originate from a state of completely witless human auto-pilot."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Jacob places this personal add at the newspaper where he works:<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reviews/97567ddc-d97f-46e0-9e20-b1f9c85e6ff5_zps4d25f8f5.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391471919i/8394885._SX540_.png" alt=" photo 97567ddc-d97f-46e0-9e20-b1f9c85e6ff5_zps4d25f8f5.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Beatrice answers his add on whim... <br><br>It's fate bringing these two Siamese soul lovers together and what a couple they are. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I feel like we grew in the same womb or something. Like we've been connected from the beginning by blood and veins. Siamese soul lovers..."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Beatrice, the narrator just doesn't quite fit in. She doesn't fit in with her family, she's never fit in her relationships and she certainly doesn't fit in Los Angeles. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>'I always felt like I didn't marry into the landscape of the human world like others did, that I was on the outside looking in.'</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Jacob believes everyone is searching for something:<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reviews/god-shaped-hole_zpsbd8ed8bc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391473236i/8394999.jpg" alt=" photo god-shaped-hole_zpsbd8ed8bc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I believe Beatrice finally finds with Jacob the place she fits and Jacob finds in Beatrice that missing peice. I can't think of a couple more suited for each other and it's one of the many things which make this book so utterly amazing. This is a must read! This is the best book I've read so far this year and I know it's early but it wouldn't surprise me if it's the best book I read all year long. It's THAT good. I simply love this couple....<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You're the world's muse, Trixie."<br>"I just want to be your muse."<br>"Done."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I should probably add this one had me crying like a baby. My friend said the only way to get me to cry while reading a book is to run over my foot while I'm reading. So I would definitely recommend some Kleenex. I know I'll always hold this one dear to my heart and I'll never get over it.<br><br><b>
  <i>"And no matter what anybody says about grief, and about time healing all wounds, the truth is, there are certain sorrows that never fade away until the heart stops beating..."</i>
</b><br><br>I would like say a special thank you to Kelly for buddy reading this one with me and for her and Jahayra being there at 2 in morning while I was sobbing so hard I could barely see to read the last 5%. Even though I know you were crying over your spilled milk Kelly ;-) <br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12317902566833806789"><b>5+++++ Outstanding stars</b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Oh hell how do I review a book like this?? I simply don't per-se I'm going give you my thoughts but honestly you need to read this with no assumptions of what its about just ignore what everyone's said and READ IT!! this is good stuff.</i>

</a><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"here's the thing," Jacob continued, "I feel like we grew in the same womb or something. Like we've been connected from the beginning by blood and veins. Siamese soul lovers. If </blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText12317902566833806789" style="display:none"><b>5+++++ Outstanding stars</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Oh hell how do I review a book like this?? I simply don't per-se I'm going give you my thoughts but honestly you need to read this with no assumptions of what its about just ignore what everyone's said and READ IT!! this is good stuff.</i>
</b><br><br><br><i>Jacob puts an ad in the paper</i><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/God-shaped%20hole%20Tiffanie%20DeBartolo%20/909C156D-9ABF-46FC-A4B8-DA69C674CF7F_zpsxrxd14t1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <blockquote>"here's the thing," Jacob continued, "I feel like we grew in the same womb or something. Like we've been connected from the beginning by blood and veins. Siamese soul lovers. If there could ever be such a thing."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br>If there ever was a couple that were meant for one another these two ARE IT!!! Trixie doesn't exactly connect closely with her friends and family she's a loner she does have people in her life but not people I would say that are close by any means but she is a strong, Jacob does have friends and his mum who he's close to but still he's the kind of person that is a league of his own, he's all about the soul and together they live in their little bubble together from day to day, moment to moment, experience to experience. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/God-shaped%20hole%20Tiffanie%20DeBartolo%20/A9603A24-DBAF-42DE-8A94-5318382F340B_zpsqv4ljo9z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392122404i/8503873._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo A9603A24-DBAF-42DE-8A94-5318382F340B_zpsqv4ljo9z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>This is the kind of story that will make you FEEL, will make you think about life, it will gut you, make you laugh, make you cry, this is a story about LOVE</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Do you believe in fate? I am a firm believer in things happen for a reason, I do believe in fate and yes I do also believe in God is that right or wrong? Well I don't think there's a right or wrong answer to that, that's just my point of view. But this story sure made me think about my life, made me thankful for what I have, make me glad I have the people who are in it, IN IT, and question what direction I'm going. And tell my family I love them every day. THIS STORY WILL MAKE YOU FEEL</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/819FCE3C-4F8C-4302-85ED-0265ED136794_zps5fc7mqxx.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392122404ra/8503874.gif" alt=" photo 819FCE3C-4F8C-4302-85ED-0265ED136794_zps5fc7mqxx.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/God-shaped%20hole%20Tiffanie%20DeBartolo%20/0C786F4E-C756-4B39-A14D-2E4CACFB905D_zpstzsbp2by.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392122404i/8503875._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0C786F4E-C756-4B39-A14D-2E4CACFB905D_zpstzsbp2by.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"It's all about now," he said. "Let's always try to remember how we feel right now."</blockquote>
</b><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/6C78C4A6-5171-4D9C-8346-3BABB3B04F70_zpssqwfxrpu.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392113509ra/8502526.gif" alt=" photo 6C78C4A6-5171-4D9C-8346-3BABB3B04F70_zpssqwfxrpu.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/i%20love%20you/068B2380-86CE-4D5E-AB23-05595D76948A_zpsgobwp8od.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392122404i/8503876._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 068B2380-86CE-4D5E-AB23-05595D76948A_zpsgobwp8od.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>The writing</b><br><br>This author is outstanding, she has a way that will pull you in and take hold of your emotions, it's exquisite, it's like poetry in many ways, she writes emotion but she also wowed me and made me laugh. <br><br><br><b>A highly recommended read I now need to read How to kill a rock star</b> <br><br>p.s Thank you Shannon for your review and for pushing me in the right direction I probably wouldn't off picked it up for a good while otherwise... so cheers your the best &lt;3<br><br>And lastly I will always love this song now for new reasons beautiful... <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=y8AWFf7EAc4">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=y8AWFf...</a><br><br><b>That is all</b><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/835316383?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer835316383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2407830084560404490"><b>4 ~ 4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391539945i/8408067._SX540_.jpg' width='390' height='451' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I’m in awe on how truly gifted of a writer Tiffanie DeBartolo actually is. <i>How to Kill a Rock Star</i> is one of my all-time favorite reads but, I was apprehensive about the synopsis for this story. I knew the writing would be too wonderful to skip any story put out by this author so I jumped in.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>”When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone. ”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Even though the synopsis threatened <b>soul mate separation</b>, I knew the journey would</span>
  <span id="freeText2407830084560404490" style="display:none"><b>4 ~ 4.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391539945i/8408067._SX540_.jpg" width="390" height="451" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m in awe on how truly gifted of a writer Tiffanie DeBartolo actually is. <i>How to Kill a Rock Star</i> is one of my all-time favorite reads but, I was apprehensive about the synopsis for this story. I knew the writing would be too wonderful to skip any story put out by this author so I jumped in.<br><br><b>
  <i>”When I was twelve, a fortune teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone. ”</i>
</b><br><br>Even though the synopsis threatened <b>soul mate separation</b>, I knew the journey would be unforgettable. The author did hook me from the start. I <b>LOVED </b> Beatrice and Jacob, they were funny, sexy, and meant to be. <br> <br><b>
  <i>“Here’s the thing. I feel like we grew in the same womb or something. Like we’ve been connected from the beginning by blood and veins. Siamese soul lovers, if there could ever be such a thing.”</i>
</b><br><br>So here I am on board with this amazing couple enjoying their highs and lows, meeting their parents, friends and although the damn fortune teller’s prediction was playing on repeat in the back of my head the entire read, I thought to myself, this is Tiffanie DeBartolo anything can happen in her books.<br><br><b>
  <i>“We had pathetically simple dreams:<br>to do meaningful work that we could be proud of, to be together, and to be happy.”</i>
</b><br><br>Sadly, what I feared that would happen did happen. It actually happened exactly like I thought it would. The idea of a twist or something extra for me didn’t happen. The story ending was straight forward. There wasn’t any magic or more. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[How hard could it have been to at least have had Jacob’s book dedication incorporated at the end?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Overall, a fairly predictable, well written read of two phenomenal characters that will always hold a special place in my heart!<br><br><b>
  <i>“The days will always be brighter because he existed.<br>The nights will always be darker because he's gone.”</i>
</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391546497ra/8408825.gif" width="320" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12839092909667765600"><b>***** 6+++ My Favorite Book Ever Stars*****</b><br/><br/><br/>I read God-Shaped Hole a few days ago and been thinking about it non-stop, to the point of obsession. Tiffanie DeBartolo rocked my world with this amazing novel, and there's nothing I can say in my review that can make justice of how magical this book was.<br/><br/>This is the most special love story I ever had the honor of reading Trixie and Jacob capture my heart and they will live there forever!!<br/><br/> <b>
  <i>If your intentions are pure,<br/> I'm seeking a friend<br/> for the end</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText12839092909667765600" style="display:none"><b>***** 6+++ My Favorite Book Ever Stars*****</b><br /><br /><br />I read God-Shaped Hole a few days ago and been thinking about it non-stop, to the point of obsession. Tiffanie DeBartolo rocked my world with this amazing novel, and there's nothing I can say in my review that can make justice of how magical this book was.<br /><br />This is the most special love story I ever had the honor of reading Trixie and Jacob capture my heart and they will live there forever!!<br /><br /> <b>
  <i>If your intentions are pure,<br /> I'm seeking a friend<br /> for the end<br /> of the world </i>
</b> <br /><br />That simple yet significant verse was all it took for Beatrice and Jacob to find each other. Their love was pure, raw and poetic. Very early on they realized it and they weren't willing to spend one minute without the other, it was not instant it was honest, no games no tricks simply love.<br /><br />The magnificence of the words written in this book took hold of my soul and made me fall in love with this characters and their story, I laughed, dreamed and cry with them. I was transported to their world, it opened me up and made me question myself but most amazingly I felt inspired beyond belief, so I invite everybody to be brave and experience the beauty of God-Shaped Hole.<br /><br />My Playlist while reading this book:<br />*Ghosts That we Knew by Mumford and Sons<br />*Paradise by Coldplay<br />*Lovers eyes By Mumford and Sons<br />*What if By Joshua Radin<br /><br /> </span>

<div id="review_543631407" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/543631407" />
    <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe"><img alt="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431962494p2/9909997.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/543631407?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe">Kim  *Mo Chridhe*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=pinnacle-of-perfection">pinnacle-of-perfection</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=books-that-made-me-cry">books-that-made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=favourites-and-obsessions">favourites-and-obsessions</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer543631407" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4045043193257861972">I have a new religion and it's called <b>Tiffaniedebartoloism</b>.<br/><br/>This is what my copy of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/248103.God_Shaped_Hole' title='God Shaped Hole by Tiffanie DeBartolo' rel='nofollow noopener'>God Shaped Hole</a> looks like.<br/><a href='http://s1275.photobucket.com/albums/y459/rebellingagainstfolding/?action=view&current=D343D24C-F8B2-4491-AA60-9186250DBE23-2148-000002E4E21A43D0_zpsec4b4365.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410798i/805994._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Please overlook the fact that I've physically highlighted the book. I know it's a sacrilegious act for some. My constant use of e-readers with their highlighting, bookmarking and note-jotting capabilities is to blame. I would have had swirly notes of my thoughts all over the pages had I not planned to lend this book but I figured, it's too good not to share. Anyway, the point of that</span>
  <span id="freeText4045043193257861972" style="display:none">I have a new religion and it's called <b>Tiffaniedebartoloism</b>.<br><br>This is what my copy of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/248103.God_Shaped_Hole" title="God Shaped Hole by Tiffanie DeBartolo" rel="nofollow noopener">God Shaped Hole</a> looks like.<br><a href="http://s1275.photobucket.com/albums/y459/rebellingagainstfolding/?action=view&amp;current=D343D24C-F8B2-4491-AA60-9186250DBE23-2148-000002E4E21A43D0_zpsec4b4365.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410798i/805994._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Please overlook the fact that I've physically highlighted the book. I know it's a sacrilegious act for some. My constant use of e-readers with their highlighting, bookmarking and note-jotting capabilities is to blame. I would have had swirly notes of my thoughts all over the pages had I not planned to lend this book but I figured, it's too good not to share. Anyway, the point of that image is to declare the fact that it is now tied with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/113791.How_to_Kill_a_Rock_Star" title="How to Kill a Rock Star by Tiffanie DeBartolo" rel="nofollow noopener">How to Kill a Rock Star</a> as my most-highlighted book ever. It helps that the main characters are writers and artists, otherwise, certain passages might have come across as corny. To me, personally, this book spoke a LOT of truths. <br><br><b>What is it with this author and her writing?</b> I can't even say that I found the story to be perfect. I even knew what would happen in the ending, thanks to the glowing <i>"This generation's <u>Love Story</u>" - Kirkus Reviews</i> printed in the cover. It can't be more obvious than that. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Still, I cried and grieved and wished for an extra hundred pages to magically appear so that I can get more Trixie and Jacob, even if I only get flashbacks and memories. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Funnily enough, I don't even feel emotionally manipulated. All I thought the entire time I read this was that I've never encountered another author who was as in touch with his/her loneliness as much as Tiffanie Debartolo was. It was laid out page after page, song after song (and there were plenty of titles scattered throughout the book.) It's one of those books you wish you had read when you were at that phase in your life when you felt all alone and no one understood you. You find comfort in the fact that something written relates to you and your feelings and vice versa. <br><br>Obviously I'm not gonna be able to write a decent review or even give an idea of what this book is about. The book blurb can do the latter. I'm too affected to do the former. I just recommend that you read it. <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4045043193257861972" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15516251931886103142">4.5 Stars. I would give it 5 but I hated the ending!! <br/><br/><b>
  <i> "When I was twelve, a fortune-teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone..."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Now when a book starts off this way you know you are in for it....But what will happen? The suspense! Agh!! I love it when a book moves/affects me and this one certainly did. I felt their love, joy, pain...<br/><br/>The book begins when Trixie answers a personal ad that Jacob placed in the newspaper.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408734i/799822.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>They meet up and really hit it off rather</span>
  <span id="freeText15516251931886103142" style="display:none">4.5 Stars. I would give it 5 but I hated the ending!! <br><br><b>
  <i> "When I was twelve, a fortune-teller told me that my one true love would die young and leave me all alone..."</i>
</b><br><br>Now when a book starts off this way you know you are in for it....But what will happen? The suspense! Agh!! I love it when a book moves/affects me and this one certainly did. I felt their love, joy, pain...<br><br>The book begins when Trixie answers a personal ad that Jacob placed in the newspaper.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408734i/799822.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They meet up and really hit it off rather quickly. They know there is some sort of spark that they are meant to be. They are both rather awkward and funny but work so great together.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mi620oxG5q1r1lmsjo6_r2_250_zps96ea1614.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><br>They both have father issues and help each other try to work through those during their journey. His father is an alcoholic and her father left her mother for another woman. Their father issues tend to cause issues with the two of them as well. The book continues as their relationship progresses and they go through many different things. There are many passages in this book that are laughable but at the same time so deep and emotional in the feelings behind them.<br><br><br>When it got to the major part in the book where everything goes down, I was:<br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mk5se5GVf61qe04alo1_250_zpsedec9d2a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I feel that I need another chapter or something. <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ What happened to Trixie?   <i>Favorite quotes<br><br>“Just knowing you exist changed the world for me.” <br><br>"Commiting suicide so as not to be murdered is the worst reason I've ever heard of to die."<br><br>"I was imploding in spirit. Real annihilation happens from the inside out."<br><br>"When I didn't hear back from God, I wheeled-and-dealed with the smaller people: Mary, Jesus, Joseph, Saint Anthony, Saint Frances, Saint Joan, Saint Michael, Saint Christopher, Adam, Eve, Matthew, Mark, Luke, John.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_423005298" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/423005298" />
    <a title="Brenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna"><img alt="Brenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580475762p2/12928663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/423005298?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=top-top-fave">top-top-fave</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer423005298" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8993136763030672399"><i>
  <b>"Sometimes the most consequential moments in my life originate from a state of completely witless human autopilot."</b>
</i><br/><br/>And... that is how the story of Beatrice & Jacob begins. On a whim, Beatrice, for a reason she herself can't even understand, decides to respond to a personal ad. <i>"If your intentions are pure I am seeking a friend for the end of the world."</i> <br/><br/>Beatrice, or <b>"Trixie"</b> as Jacob affectionately calls her, is the voice of this story. She is sick of the LA lifestyle and is always let down </span>
  <span id="freeText8993136763030672399" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"Sometimes the most consequential moments in my life originate from a state of completely witless human autopilot."</b>
</i><br /><br />And... that is how the story of Beatrice &amp; Jacob begins. On a whim, Beatrice, for a reason she herself can't even understand, decides to respond to a personal ad. <i>"If your intentions are pure I am seeking a friend for the end of the world."</i> <br /><br />Beatrice, or <b>"Trixie"</b> as Jacob affectionately calls her, is the voice of this story. She is sick of the LA lifestyle and is always let down by men. She has a witty, but cynical charm about her, that I loved (most of the time).<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I didn't know how to act like a normal person and be in love at the same time."</i>
</b><br /><br />What really made the book for me though, was <b>Jacob</b> *sigh* he is one of the most interesting characters I've encountered in a book. There are too many adjectives to describe him. He is "raggedly, poetically handsome," a dreamer, a romantic, spontaneous, eccentric, intense, passionate, sweet, soulful, deep. I could go on and on. Jacob's best friend, Pete describes him perfectly...<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"He wants someone to obsess over, someone to possess his soul, and those are his corny words, by the way, not mine. It's what he lives for. It's what he thinks life's all about. Do you get what I'm saying?"</b>
</i><br /><br />Immediately, Trixie and Jacob have an extremely intense connection. They just get each other. This wasn't a simple case of "insta-love" (that can drive me nuts) though. I could literally <i>feel</i> their connection from the first meet all the way to the last page of the book, it was INTENSE. I have loved a lot of couples in books before and have obsessed over characters and rooted for them and wanted so badly for them to be together. But this was a new and different experience for me. The couple <u>IS</u> together for pretty much the <i>entire</i> time. It's their love story and daily life over years. We get to enjoy them, get to know them, and go through many ups and downs. I can honestly say that I haven't ever <i>felt</i> the love between two characters like I did with Trixie and Jacob. I can't even explain it properly, I just felt it. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"A search. We're all searching to fill up what I like to call that big, God-shaped hole in our souls."</i>
</b><br /><br />I wish I could have read this through my kindle app, because I literally would have highlighted half the book. I have a notebook for when I read print versions of books, and I have <b>pages and pages</b> full of quotes. I was <b>hooked and completely intrigued</b> from the very beginning.This book had me feeling every emotion imaginable. I was laughing (and laughing <b>a lot</b>) one second and sobbing the next. I don't know how she does it, but Tiffanie DeBartolo can bring emotion out of me like no other. She is an incredibly brilliant writer. Her voice is so distinct and unique. I found alot of similarites between this and her other novel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/113791.How_to_Kill_a_Rock_Star" title="How to Kill a Rock Star by Tiffanie DeBartolo" rel="nofollow noopener">How to Kill a Rock Star</a> (top 5 book for me &amp; this REALLY made me want to re-read immediately) with the atypical hero of the stories, the music references, and the soulfulness. I sincerely hope she comes back to writing and publishes another novel. She is too amazing not to. <br /><br />I <b>highly</b> recommend this book to people who enjoy a great, realistic, <i>very</i> emotional love story. It is a beautiful story that I am so grateful I read. It made me think differently about life in a lot of ways. That's a pretty big deal, I think.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"We had pathetically simple dreams: to do meaningful work that we could be proud of, to be together, and to be happy. That wasn't too much to ask. Or was it?"</i>
</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8993136763030672399" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_679078752" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/679078752" />
    <a title="S.R. Grey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10599127-s-r-grey"><img alt="S.R. Grey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585422853p2/10599127.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/679078752?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.R. Grey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.R. Grey" href="/user/show/10599127-s-r-grey">S.R. Grey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=poetic-writing">poetic-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=more-than-5-stars-deserved">more-than-5-stars-deserved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=not-like-anything-else">not-like-anything-else</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=no-cliffhanger">no-cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=pageturner">pageturner</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=hardtoputdown">hardtoputdown</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=cantwaittostart">cantwaittostart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=getoutyourhighlighter">getoutyourhighlighter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10599127-s-r-grey?shelf=wellwritten">wellwritten</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer679078752" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6861306342882437104">Wow! Please don't be put off by all the "this is sad", "this is depressing" reviews. Yes, there is sadness in the novel. And not gonna lie, the end is depressing. BUT God-Shaped Hole is so much more than a tragic tale of loss. Let's review, shall we... <br/><br/>First, we meet two fabulously unique characters, Jacob Grace (loved him) and Beatrice "Trixie" Jordan. They are quirky and different and you never doubt these two are meant to be together. And, except for one hiccup in their time together, neither</span>
  <span id="freeText6861306342882437104" style="display:none">Wow! Please don't be put off by all the "this is sad", "this is depressing" reviews. Yes, there is sadness in the novel. And not gonna lie, the end is depressing. BUT God-Shaped Hole is so much more than a tragic tale of loss. Let's review, shall we... <br><br>First, we meet two fabulously unique characters, Jacob Grace (loved him) and Beatrice "Trixie" Jordan. They are quirky and different and you never doubt these two are meant to be together. And, except for one hiccup in their time together, neither do they. <br><br><a href="http://s925.photobucket.com/user/xlavendermoonx/media/tumblr_m5bjt9z2KW1r1ivb5o1_500_zpsa3dd8fcc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430823ra/863942.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m5bjt9z2KW1r1ivb5o1_500_zpsa3dd8fcc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They live, they love...<br><br><a href="http://s925.photobucket.com/user/xlavendermoonx/media/tumblr_m8frgv7uHR1qzgcaoo1_500_zpsec7dc8fa.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380426472ra/852209.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m8frgv7uHR1qzgcaoo1_500_zpsec7dc8fa.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They dream, they plan...<br><br><a href="http://s925.photobucket.com/user/xlavendermoonx/media/tumboriginal_zps6aef7e30.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430823ra/863943.gif" alt=" photo tumboriginal_zps6aef7e30.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But all along you as the reader (and Jacob and Trixie, in a way, as well) know this can't last. And it doesn't. (not a spoiler, I think it's pretty clear there is no HEA in GSH). This is also where I suggest you have lots of tissues on hand. You, as the reader, will go through every heart-wrenching emotion along with Trixie. And prepare to be gutted. But remember: <br><br><a href="http://s925.photobucket.com/user/xlavendermoonx/media/tumbacceptancehope_zps251fb6e3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430823ra/863944.gif" alt=" photo tumbacceptancehope_zps251fb6e3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is a light at the end of the very dark tunnel. Trixie comes out a better person for having known Jacob Grace. She finds strength and hope, strength to follow her heart, hope to believe there is a future...for her. <br><br><a href="http://s925.photobucket.com/user/xlavendermoonx/media/tumbhope_zps58be8e65.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380430823i/863945.jpg" alt=" photo tumbhope_zps58be8e65.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So, please, whatever you do, take time out to read this novel! You'll laugh, you'll cry. You will FEEL! And hopefully in the end it will all be worth it. <br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6861306342882437104" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743499286?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa" href="/user/show/9684061-melissa">Melissa</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743499286" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1179877019705039530">Wow.... another great book from Tiffanie DeBartolo. I am in awe of the amazing stories and characters that she's created. <i> How To Kill A Rockstar</i> was one of the best books I have ever read and <i>GSH</i> has definitely been added to my favorites list.<br/><br/>I loved that Trixie and Jacob met in such a quirky and unique way and had such a strong "siamese soul lovers" connection right from the start. The whole book was deep and heartfelt and it even made me assess my own life. I was heartbroken over the ending, </span>
  <span id="freeText1179877019705039530" style="display:none">Wow.... another great book from Tiffanie DeBartolo. I am in awe of the amazing stories and characters that she's created. <i> How To Kill A Rockstar</i> was one of the best books I have ever read and <i>GSH</i> has definitely been added to my favorites list.<br /><br />I loved that Trixie and Jacob met in such a quirky and unique way and had such a strong "siamese soul lovers" connection right from the start. The whole book was deep and heartfelt and it even made me assess my own life. I was heartbroken over the ending, but isn't that how life is most of the time, unexpected?<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"If your intentions are pure<br />I'm seeking a friend<br />for the end <br />of the world"</b>
  </i>
  <blockquote>
    <br />
  </blockquote>
</blockquote></span>

<div id="review_2381420204" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2381420204" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2381420204?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34139890-god-shaped-hole">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2381420204" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9582248664798211447"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1525413412i/25478645._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>‘…memories are the patches that make up the quilt of our emotions. A beautiful way to put it, but wrong. If that were true, then memories would blanket us, they would keep us warm. My memories were chilling me to the bone.’</b><br/><br/>Oh our hearts. <b>We are wrecked! </b>Wrecked we tell you. We’ve recently overhauled our blog and in doing so, discovered we had never reviewed God Shaped Hole. This is one of our favourite books, and we couldn’t do it justice without once again experiencing the provocative words of</span>
  <span id="freeText9582248664798211447" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1525413412i/25478645._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>‘…memories are the patches that make up the quilt of our emotions. A beautiful way to put it, but wrong. If that were true, then memories would blanket us, they would keep us warm. My memories were chilling me to the bone.’</b><br><br>Oh our hearts. <b>We are wrecked! </b>Wrecked we tell you. We’ve recently overhauled our blog and in doing so, discovered we had never reviewed God Shaped Hole. This is one of our favourite books, and we couldn’t do it justice without once again experiencing the provocative words of Tiffanie De Bartolo, so we decided to do a re-read. There was a little hesitation as we wondered if we would experience the level of emotion we did when we first devoured it over 5 years ago.<br><br><b>‘But I guessed that no matter how strong it was, love alone couldn’t turn a speck of dust into a galaxy of stars.’</b><br><br>Well, we needn’t have worried because the answer was a resounding <b>yes!</b> All the feelings we experienced <b>then,</b> were just as prevalent <b>now.</b> There’s so much to say about this book, but then to say too much would impact on how you experience the evolution and conclusion of Trixie and Jacob’s intense, aching and beautiful love story. These two were the epitome of soulmate love.<br><br>Tiffanie De Bartolo’s writing is breathtaking. Just as in To Kill A Rockstar, one of our all-time top favourite reads, this author delivers words that impact your life and heart with what appears to be a natural and effortless talent. Her words are poetic, profound, thought provoking, honest and sincere. Nothing is sugar coated, we get a warts and all look at a love that’s intense, organic, beautiful and flawed, through the stunning prose. Her musings via Trixie left us shaking our heads in awe.<br><br><b>‘It seemed cruelly unfair to me, even then, how fast your life can change before you have an opportunity to rethink your choices. We should get second chances on the big stuff. We should come equipped with erasers attached to the tops of our heads. Like pencils. We should be able to flip over and scribble away mistakes, at least once or twice during the duration of our existence, especially in matters of life and death.’</b><br><br>Emotions are at an optimum during our time spent with Trixie and Jacob because at a point Tiffanie De Bartolo draws us into Trixie and Jacob’s life and love experiences and these guys ceased to be characters, instead they felt like people we know, people we care about and people we love.<br><br><b>‘.. you can’t put life on pause and then catch up with it later when you have more energy to give. You have to play it all the way through to the end.’</b><br><br>The synopsis summarises everything you need to know about the story so we won’t expand on that except to say, Jacob and Trixie’s happiness made us euphoric, their disappointments decimated, and we felt every emotion in between with them as they circumnavigated the ups and downs of their new found love. OMG! We suffered at times, our hearts really did hurt.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Don’t waste your time with fear….fear won’t keep you safe from being hurt.”</i>
</b><br><br>The music which exudes from every pore of the author in her writing, once again plays a role in God Shaped Hole, relating moments to song and making each moment personal.<br><br>The second read was as painful, fun, emotional and as tortuous as the first, and we enjoyed every feeling this author elicited from us. Nothing was spared in this achingly beautiful exploration of true soulmate love, dreams, fate, and we wouldn’t want it to be.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Just knowing you exist changed the world for me.”</i>
</b><br><br>After our re-read, we’re <i>okay</i>….well,<i> we think </i>we’re okay. One thing we know for sure, book world needs more Tiffanie De Bartolo stories, two just aren’t enough! Do yourselves a favour, and <b>1click </b> this book now!<br><br><b>God Shaped Hole is currently on sale!<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">my link text</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">my link text</a></b><br><br><b>Come visit and follow us at:</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462588446i/19017616._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>✲ <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✲ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✲ <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✲ <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9582248664798211447" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=audio-2018">audio-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=fast-connection">fast-connection</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=annoying">annoying</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=heroine-meh">heroine-meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=disappointed">disappointed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=mental-health-rep">mental-health-rep</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=strong-woman">strong-woman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=womens-fiction">womens-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=2018-read">2018-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18967379-bookphenomena-micky?shelf=audio">audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1397533990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6050271342071947686">I’m going to keep this short as I offend lovers of this book left, right and centre.<br/><br/>Clearly, I am cold, unfeeling fish. This to me, was 90% of fairly boring relationship (I’ve no idea how I kept going, other than it became a challenge I wanted to win), then 10% of stupid outcome that I kind of expected. I felt nothing, I didn’t hurt and I hated the speedy wrap-up. I did like the writing style.<br/><br/>Good narration.<br/><br/>I’m glad it’s done and hopefully I’ll never have to think about this book again.</span>

          </span>
        </div>
