<div id="review_1050091864" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1050091864" />
    <a title="Amber Rose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11143936-amber-rose"><img alt="Amber Rose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1356721991p2/11143936.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1050091864?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amber Rose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amber Rose" href="/user/show/11143936-amber-rose">Amber Rose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18952257-god-shaped-hole">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11143936-amber-rose?shelf=my-favorites">my-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11143936-amber-rose?shelf=standalones">standalones</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1050091864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12749163732621109280"><a href='http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/5stars_zpscf7811d0.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410658783i/11137173.png' alt=' photo 5stars_zpscf7811d0.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> <blockquote> “Don't waste your time with fear.. Fear won't keep you safe from being hurt.” </blockquote> </b> <br/><br/><a href='http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/God-ShapedHole_zps937f799c.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410658783i/11137174._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo God-ShapedHole_zps937f799c.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>This book blew my mind. I am not even sure how to express how much this book tore me apart. It fucked my world up let me put it like that. I loved the authors book, How to Kill a Rock Star. I knew starting this book that I should not take this story likely. I knew what would happen. It was just a given. It is read out and expressed to you many times through out the book. How could I not, NOT want to read it</span>
  <span id="freeText12749163732621109280" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/5stars_zpscf7811d0.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410658783i/11137173.png" alt=" photo 5stars_zpscf7811d0.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> <blockquote> “Don't waste your time with fear.. Fear won't keep you safe from being hurt.” </blockquote> </b> <br><br><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/God-ShapedHole_zps937f799c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410658783i/11137174._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo God-ShapedHole_zps937f799c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This book blew my mind. I am not even sure how to express how much this book tore me apart. It fucked my world up let me put it like that. I loved the authors book, How to Kill a Rock Star. I knew starting this book that I should not take this story likely. I knew what would happen. It was just a given. It is read out and expressed to you many times through out the book. How could I not, NOT want to read it. <br><br>This author is a magical writer. Nothing paranormal or anything like that. It's more poetic that is for sure. She captures the characters in a magical way and the love they have for each other is internal. True love, soul mates type of shit. And I felt that to my gut. I knew these two are one of a fucking kind and I am glad they shared their experience with me. The bond these two have makes the love that I know just love. This type of love they have is that one truly once in a lifetime experience. Their made for each other. That's what made this book too. The characters were the most brilliant fucking<br>characters I have read in a long time. There is not a single type of character like, Jacob and Trixie. <br><br><b> <blockquote> “You try and act so tough, you think you're so damn hopeless and godless and faithless, but you don't fool me. People without hope aren't tormented by the world the way you are. People without hope don't give a shit. but I see it in you, in the way you look at things, even in the way you look at me sometimes, like I'm the coolest fucking guy in the universe, and I know it's in there. Reverence. Belief. Something. You have a lot more faith than you own up to. You just don't want to be let down. But I'm not going to let you down again. Not if I can help it.” </blockquote> </b> <br><br><a href="http://s1321.photobucket.com/user/ambersreadingroom/media/GodShapedHoles_zpsc46c8887.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410658783i/11137175._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo GodShapedHoles_zpsc46c8887.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It breaks my fucking heart into little pieces and wanted to throw my kindle across the highway (since I was riding in car), I really had it planned in my mind, I was going to roll down my window and say <b> FUCK YOU WORLD!!! </b> I am still thinking about it while I am laying here in the hotel room bed. If I could open the window I would just throw it out the window and hope the fucking buss station across the street hits my kindle and drags little pieces of it all the way to California.<br><br>I don't know how I am going to get over this book. I don't think I can. It has left it's imprint in my heart and soul. Its the type of book that leave its mark and I will keep thinking about it over and over for next...forever.... I am seriously getting fucking teary eye just thinking about this book and looking through my clippings for quotes I want to use. <br><br>I kind of want to lock this book away so no one can have the same type of feelings I have for these characters. I want to keep them for my self. But, then again I want to share my experience with anyone who can handle this type of book. Someone who can appreciate the type of beautiful writing you will get in this book. Enjoy the words flowing into something so beautiful <br>that it will grow and make you think there is nothing better then this right now. Its a wonderful feeling and I thank this author for creating something so perfect. <br><br><b> <blockquote> “Thoughts are king, Trixie, king!” </blockquote> </b> <br><br>Were their flaws? Hell yes. But those didn't matter to me after I read this. It wasn't the type of flaws that made me want to lower the book rating or anything. There was angst, punching bitches in the face moments. Fuck I need a snickers right now... My heart hurts. In a good way and in a broken in little pieces way. But it doesn't matter because there is a man <br>called, Jacob in this book. And, Jacob deserves fucking everything in this goddamn world.... He's my everything right now. <br><br><b> <blockquote> “If your intentions are pure, I'm seeking a friend for the end of the world.” </blockquote> </b> <br><br><a href="http://www.thereadingroomblog.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461870048i/18922777.png" alt=" photo Follow the Readng Rom Blog_zpsznrkrqks.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/thereadingroombookblog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1461870152i/18922804.png" alt=" photo Like the Reading ROom Blog on Fb_zpsnigjcua7.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12749163732621109280" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/313401910" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/313401910?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer313401910" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer406791495789670821">It has been almost a year since I first read this, and it still haunts me. <br/><br/><i>“It seemed cruelly unfair to me, even then, how fast your life can change before you have an opportunity to rethink your choices. We should get second chances on the big stuff. We should come equipped with erasers attached to the tops of our heads. Like pencils. We should be able to flip over and scribble away mistakes, at least once or twice during the duration of our existence, especially in matters of life and death.”</i> </span>
  <span id="freeText406791495789670821" style="display:none">It has been almost a year since I first read this, and it still haunts me. <br><br><i>“It seemed cruelly unfair to me, even then, how fast your life can change before you have an opportunity to rethink your choices. We should get second chances on the big stuff. We should come equipped with erasers attached to the tops of our heads. Like pencils. We should be able to flip over and scribble away mistakes, at least once or twice during the duration of our existence, especially in matters of life and death.”</i> <br><br>There really isn't much more I can say. It's a devastatingly beautiful story, one that I will never forget.<br><br><a href="http://s1313.photobucket.com/user/bwsmith816/media/jeff-buckley_zps0ba7eeb6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375205i/729738.jpg" alt=" photo jeff-buckley_zps0ba7eeb6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AK8AMLQ14C6RBB2/oTVmPxCoxkjBe4sSEDvUbR8KbeLReVvILlESaWbxRs6LiX76zwiOmT8deATH0UW7KRQpyg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NFGYy3dEG+FBkI/A1RHxfPNJyGS360ZeX3Eg8S8sPGPlh8Mz7SDpprZl1LH/rem5LOmAtUmNtUiIm7EnGTJ4Sw==')})
  }
//]]>

Forced to reach out to her last resort, Beyah has to spend the remainder of her summer on a peninsula in Texas with a father she barely knows. Beyah\'s plan is to keep her head down and let the summer slip by seamlessly, but her new neighbor Samson throws a wrench in that plan.\n\nSamson and Beyah have nothing in common on the surface.\n\nShe comes from a life of poverty and neglect; he comes from a family of wealth and privilege. But one thing they do have in common is that they\'re both drawn to sad things. Which means they\'re drawn to each other. With an almost immediate connection too intense for them to continue denying, Beyah and Samson agree to stay in the shallow end of a summer fling. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1770347680711636455">Tiffanie DeBartolo's most recent novel is Sorrow. Her previous novels include God Shaped Hole (2002), How To Kill a Rock Star (2005), and the graphic novel Grace: Based on the Jeff Buckley Story (2019). She also wrote and directed the film Dream for an Insomniac (1996) starring Jennifer Aniston and Ione Skye. <br/>Tiffanie is the founder and CEO of San Francisco Bay Area record label Bright Antenna, wh</span>
  <span id="freeText1770347680711636455" style="display:none">Tiffanie DeBartolo's most recent novel is Sorrow. Her previous novels include God Shaped Hole (2002), How To Kill a Rock Star (2005), and the graphic novel Grace: Based on the Jeff Buckley Story (2019). She also wrote and directed the film Dream for an Insomniac (1996) starring Jennifer Aniston and Ione Skye. <br />Tiffanie is the founder and CEO of San Francisco Bay Area record label Bright Antenna, whose roster of artists include The Wombats, Wilderado, Sports Team, and Prep.<br />Tiffanie is also the cofounder of the ShineMaker Foundation, a charity organization dedicated to supporting human rights, women's rights, education, animal welfare, and the environment.<br />In her spare time, she is a runner, hiker, yogi, world-traveler, cook, poet, and artist.<br />She lives in Mill Valley with her husband Scott Schumaker and her two Irish Wolfhounds, Dipsea and Kazoo.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1770347680711636455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
